  • Proactively monitoring project progress, identifying potential risks and issues, and reporting them promptly.
  • Managing and documenting changes to the project scope, and communicating their impact to clients and relevant stakeholders.
  • Ensuring projects are delivered on time, within budget, and to the agreed-upon scope.
  • Handling multiple projects and priorities simultaneously in a fast-paced environment while consistently delivering high-quality results.

  • Develop and deploy ML/DL models to support NLP/NLU tasks such as summarization, classification, and retrieval scoring.
  • Integrate vector databases, semantic search tools, and embedding models for high-performance document retrieval.
  • Work with unstructured and semi-structured data sources (PDFs, HTML, JSON, SQL, etc.).
  • Collaborate with data engineers, ML engineers, and product teams to build end-to-end generative AI solutions.
  • Monitor performance, latency, and relevance metrics; iterate on retrieval and generation models.
  • Implement prompt engineering strategies and hybrid approaches (rule-based + neural) to enhance model reliability.
  • Contribute to research and innovation in applied generative AI, and stay up-to-date with the latest in LLM, RAG, and MLOps ecosystems.

Preferred Skills:

  • Strong experience with RAG architectures and hybrid retrieval systems.
  • Solid hands-on knowledge of LLMs (e.g., GPT, Mistral, LLaMA, Claude, DeepSeek, etc.) and embedding models (e.g., SBERT, OpenAI, HuggingFace models).
  • Proficiency in machine learning / deep learning using PyTorch, TensorFlow, Hugging Face Transformers, etc.
  • Experience with vector databases (e.g., FAISS, Weaviate, Pinecone, Qdrant).
  • Experience in text chunking, retrieval scoring, prompt tuning, or LoRA/PEFT methods.
  • Strong background in NLP, information retrieval, and knowledge graphs is a plus.
  • Comfortable with Python and associated data science stacks (Pandas, NumPy, Scikit-learn).
  • Experience working with real-world messy data (PDF parsing, OCR, HTML scraping, etc.).

Lean Transitions Solutions is seeking a proactive and detail-oriented Pre-Sales Business Analyst. This role is crucial in supporting the sales cycle by translating customer needs into clear, solution-ready requirements and documentation. You will collaborate closely with the PMO Delivery Director, while also providing pre-sales support to the Strategic Business Director and Sales & Customer Success Executive. Your responsibilities will include requirement gathering, solution scoping, and preparing technical inputs for proposals and demos. The ideal candidate will ensure customer expectations are accurately understood, documented, and aligned with product capabilities before transitioning to delivery teams. This role may also involve supporting early delivery phases for smooth implementation planning.

Key Responsibilities:

  1. Pre-Sales Discovery & Requirements Gathering

    • Attend client discovery calls and demos alongside sales representatives.
    • Capture and document business needs, workflows, and functional expectations.
    • Clarify objectives, use cases, and customer challenges early in the sales cycle.
    • Translate discussions into structured requirement notes or actionable briefs.

  2. Solution Scoping & Technical Documentation

    • Develop preliminary solution outlines, scope summaries, and feature mappings.
    • Create draft Business Requirement Documents (BRDs) or Functional Specifications (FSDs) as needed.
    • Produce workflow diagrams, wireframes, or configuration concepts with designer team support (using tools like Figma, Lucidchart, Visio).
    • Align proposed solutions with product capabilities and delivery feasibility in coordination with the PMO.

  3. Proposal & Technical Input Support

    • Contribute technical and functional sections to proposals, SOWs, capability decks, and solution documentation.
    • Provide supporting materials such as feature breakdowns, workflow references, screenshots, or demo visuals.
    • Coordinate with PMs, Product Teams, and Solutions Architects to validate effort, timelines, and scope.
    • Ensure documentation libraries, templates, and proposal-related assets are current and accurate.

  4. Demo Support & Client Workshops

    • Assist in tailoring and preparing demos based on client requirements.
    • Support solution walkthroughs by demonstrating functionality, workflows, or configuration concepts.
    • Capture questions, required modifications, and follow-up actions from demos or workshops.
    • Provide functional clarity to Sales & Customer Success and Product Delivery teams.

  5. Collaboration with Sales, Marketing & Technical Teams

    • Work with the Sales & Customer Success Executive to align scope, requirements, and customer expectations.
    • Provide technical input to marketing collateral showcasing system workflows or configurations.
    • Support design and content teams with diagrams, Figma links, functionality clarifications, or feature visuals.
    • Coordinate early solution feasibility with PMO, developers, and product architects.

  6. Delivery Handover & Flexible BA Support (Post-Sale)

    • Prepare structured handover notes for PMO, BA, and delivery teams to begin implementation.
    • Clarify assumptions, workflows, deliverables, and effort during pre-kick-off activities.
    • Transition temporarily into a Business Analyst role during project initiation where needed.
    • Support configuration workshops, requirement validation, and solution alignment during onboarding.

Preferred Skills, Experience & Background:

  • Experience: 2–4 years in pre-sales, business analysis, solution consulting, or functional coordination within a software/SaaS/IT environment.
  • Team Collaboration: Experience working with delivery, product, or technical teams to translate requirements into solutions.
  • Lifecycle Familiarity: Familiarity with software implementation lifecycles and client discovery processes.

Tools & Systems:

  • Microsoft Office/365: Strong experience (Excel, PowerPoint, Word).
  • Project Tracking: Working knowledge of Jira or similar tools.
  • Diagramming/Workflow Tools: Experience using Visio, Lucidchart, Figma, Miro.

Skills & Capabilities:

  • Excellent written and verbal communication skills.
  • Ability to gather, structure, and document requirements clearly.
  • Strong analytical and problem-solving abilities.
  • Ability to collaborate effectively with cross-functional teams (Sales, PMO, Delivery).
  • Good attention to detail and ability to handle multiple priorities.

Education:

  • Bachelor’s degree in IT, Business, Engineering, Computer Science, or a related field.

Preferred Industry & Product Knowledge:

  • Exposure to Lean, manufacturing, logistics, or process improvement environments.
  • Understanding of SaaS platforms, workflow-based systems, or ERP/MES/QMS tools.

Preferred Proposal & Demo Involvement:

  • Exposure to software demos, configuration showcases, or pre-sales workshops.

Preferred Collaboration & Market Alignment:
